TITLE: Privacy Policy — Boat Rental Marbella
DESCRIPTION: Privacy policy for boatrentalinmarbella.com — what data we collect when you contact us via WhatsApp, email or the booking form, how we use it, and your GDPR rights.

Privacy Policy Last updated: 1 June 2026 This privacy policy explains how Boat Rental Marbella (operating the website boatrentalinmarbella.com , hereafter "we", "us", "the Site") collects, uses and protects your personal data when you visit the Site, contact us via WhatsApp, email or the booking form, or charter a boat through us. We comply with the EU General Data Protection Regulation (Regulation (EU) 2016/679, "GDPR") and Spanish data-protection law (LOPDGDD 3/2018). 1. Who is the data controller? The data controller for personal data collected through this Site is: Boat Rental Marbella Marbella, Andalucía, Spain (postal code 29602) WhatsApp / phone: +358 400 406 194 2. What data do we collect? We only collect data that you give us, or that is generated automatically when you browse: Booking and enquiry data — name, phone number, email address, date(s) of intended charter, group size, departure port, language preference, and any free-text message you send via the booking form, WhatsApp, email, or Instagram/Facebook DM. Payment data — for confirmed bookings, payments are processed by the boat operator's own payment provider (typically Stripe, Revolut Business, or bank transfer). We do not store full card numbers on this Site. Technical data — IP address, browser type, device type, referring page, pages viewed, and timestamps. Collected via standard server logs and Google Analytics 4 (measurement ID G-SPMRYJVTHD). Cookies — see section 7 below. 3. Why do we use it (legal basis)? To answer your enquiry and arrange your charter — legal basis: performance of a contract or pre-contractual steps at your request (GDPR art. 6(1)(b)). To share your booking with the relevant boat operator (e.g. the skipper, charter company, or marina) so they can run the trip — legal basis: contract (art. 6(1)(b)). To comply with Spanish tax and maritime law — e.g. issuing invoices, recording passenger lists where the captain requires them — legal basis: legal obligation (art. 6(1)(c)). To improve the Site and measure traffic — legal basis: legitimate interest in operating an effective website (art. 6(1)(f)), with anonymised analytics where possible. To send you marketing emails or WhatsApp messages — only with your explicit consent, which you can withdraw at any time (art. 6(1)(a)). We do not currently run a marketing newsletter. 4. Who do we share it with? We only share your data with parties that need it to deliver your charter or run the Site: The boat operator / skipper assigned to your charter (name, phone, date, group size). Payment processors (Stripe, Revolut, etc.) when you pay online. Communication providers — WhatsApp (Meta Platforms Ireland Ltd.), Gmail / Google Workspace, Instagram and Facebook (Meta) for the messages you send through those channels. Hosting and analytics — GitHub Pages (Microsoft Corp., US), Cloudflare, Google Analytics 4 (Google Ireland Ltd.). Tax authorities, insurers and law enforcement if we are legally required to do so. Some of these providers are based outside the EU/EEA (United States). Transfers rely on the EU–US Data Privacy Framework and/or the European Commission's Standard Contractual Clauses. 5. How long do we keep it? Enquiries that don't lead to a booking — deleted within 12 months. Booking records and invoices — kept for the period required by Spanish tax law (currently 6 years). Server logs and analytics — typically 14 months (Google Analytics default). Marketing consent records — until you withdraw consent, plus a reasonable archival period. 6. Your rights Under GDPR you can, at any time, ask us to: Confirm what data we hold about you and give you a copy (right of access). Correct any inaccurate or out-of-date data (right of rectification). Delete your data when it is no longer needed (right of erasure / "to be forgotten"). Restrict or object to certain processing. Receive your data in a portable format. Withdraw any consent you have given (without affecting prior lawful processing). To exercise any of these rights, message us on WhatsApp at +358 400 406 194 with a copy of an identifying document. We will reply within 30 days. If you are not satisfied with our response, you can complain to the Spanish Data Protection Agency ( Agencia Española de Protección de Datos — www.aepd.es ). 7. Cookies The Site uses a small number of cookies and similar technologies: Strictly necessary — to display the Site, remember your language choice (EN/ES) and your booking-form draft. No consent needed. Analytics — Google Analytics 4 (cookies _ga , _ga_* ) to measure visits anonymously. You can opt out at any time by installing the Google Analytics Opt-out add-on or by clearing cookies in your browser. Third-party embeds — videos hosted on this domain do not set cookies. Embedded social-media links (Instagram, Facebook, WhatsApp) only set cookies if you click them. 8. Children The Site is not directed at children under 14. We do not knowingly collect personal data from anyone under 14. Children may, of course, travel on a charter — in that case, their parent or legal guardian provides the booking data. 9. Security The Site is served over HTTPS. Data sent through WhatsApp is end-to-end encrypted by Meta. Internal records are stored in access-controlled cloud services (Google Workspace) protected by two-factor authentication. No system is 100% secure, but we apply commercially reasonable measures. 10. Changes to this policy We may update this policy from time to time — the "Last updated" date at the top will always show the current version. Material changes will be highlighted on the homepage for at least 30 days. 11. Contact Any privacy question or request: WhatsApp +358 400 406 194 . See also our Terms & Conditions .

URL: https://boatrentalinmarbella.com/puerto-banus-vs-marbella-marina-boat-rental/
TITLE: Puerto Banus vs Marbella Marina Boat Rental: Which Departure Point Is Best?
DESCRIPTION: Compare Puerto Banús vs Marbella Marina boat rental. Find which departure point suits your charter: glitz, parking, or convenience. Book your boat today.

Home › Puerto Banus vs Marbella Marina Boat Rental: Which Departure Point Is Best? When planning a boat rental in Marbella, the first decision is often where to depart from: the glitzy Puerto Banús or the more central Marbella Marina (Puerto Deportivo). Both are excellent bases for a day on the water, but they differ in atmosphere, access, and typical itineraries. This guide compares Puerto Banús vs Marbella Marina boat rental options so you can choose the departure point that matches your style. Location and Accessibility Puerto Banús sits 6 km west of Marbella town centre, near the Golden Mile and the Sierra Blanca mountains. It is a purpose-built luxury marina with a large car park (though expensive at €3–4/h) and regular bus connections from Marbella (line L-2, €1.40). Marbella Marina, by contrast, is right next to the Old Town and the Alameda Park, making it walkable from most central hotels. Parking is cheaper (€2/h) but can be tight on summer weekends. If you are staying on the Golden Mile or in Nueva Andalucía, Puerto Banús is more convenient; if you are in the Old Town, Marbella Marina wins on proximity. Atmosphere and Vibe Puerto Banús is synonymous with luxury yachts, designer boutiques, and buzzing nightlife. It is a place to see and be seen – expect supercars, champagne bars, and a glamorous crowd. Marbella Marina is more laid-back, with a traditional fishing-port feel, casual chiringuitos, and a family-friendly promenade. Your choice of departure point sets the tone for the day: Puerto Banús for a high-energy start, Marbella Marina for a relaxed, authentic Spanish experience. Boat Fleet and Departure Points All boats in our fleet depart from Puerto Banús. This means you have access to a wide range of vessels, from the Astondoa 40 (12.5m, 9 pax, €749/2h) to the Mangusta 80 (24m, 12 pax, €4,719/4h with jet ski). Marbella Marina has its own charter operators, but they are fewer in number and often have smaller fleets. If you want the biggest choice and best value, Puerto Banús is the stronger option. Browse our full fleet . Typical Itineraries from Each Marina From Puerto Banús, you can reach the exclusive coves of Cala del Faro and Cala Cortés in under 10 minutes. Heading west, you can explore the coast towards Estepona and Sotogrande. From Marbella Marina, you are closer to Cabopino (with its sand dunes) and the eastern coast towards Fuengirola. The distance between the two marinas is only 4 NM (15–20 minutes by boat), so you can easily start at one and visit the other during your charter. Cost Comparison Item Puerto Banús Marbella Marina Parking (per hour) €3–4 €2 Taxi from Marbella centre €10–15 €5–8 Bus fare €1.40 (line L-2) Walkable Boat charter (2h, Tier A) €749 Similar via other operators While parking is cheaper at Marbella Marina, the boat charter prices at Puerto Banús are competitive and include skipper, fuel, drinks, and snacks. The overall cost difference is minimal when you factor in the included extras. Which Should You Choose? If you value convenience and a lively atmosphere, and you are staying near the Golden Mile or Nueva Andalucía, choose Puerto Banús . It offers the largest fleet, direct access to the best coves, and a glamorous start to your day. If you prefer a quieter, more central location with cheaper parking and easy access to the Old Town, opt for Marbella Marina – but note you will need to book with a different operator. For most visitors, Puerto Banús is the superior choice for a boat rental in Marbella. Check availability and pricing . Frequently Asked Questions Which departure point is closer to Marbella town centre? Marbella Marina is directly adjacent to the Old Town and the Golden Mile, just a 5-minute walk from the main square. Puerto Banús is about 6 km west, a 10-minute drive or a 20-minute bus ride from the town centre. Can I park at Puerto Banús when renting a boat? Yes, Puerto Banús has several public car parks, but rates are higher – expect €3–4 per hour during summer. Marbella Marina offers cheaper parking at around €2 per hour, though spaces can be limited on weekends. Which marina has better nightlife after a boat trip? Puerto Banús is famous for its high-end nightclubs and beach clubs (e.g., Ocean Club, Pangea). Marbella Marina has a more relaxed vibe with traditional tapas bars and a few cocktail spots, but the party scene is less intense. Do all boats depart from Puerto Banús? All boats in our fleet depart from Puerto Banús. If you prefer Marbella Marina, you would need to book via a different operator. We recommend Puerto Banús for its direct access to the best coves along the Costa del Sol. Which departure point is better for a family day trip? Marbella Marina is quieter and more family-friendly, with easy access to the beach and playgrounds nearby. Puerto Banús can be busier but offers more charter options and direct routes to child-friendly coves like Cala Cortés. How far is it from Marbella Marina to Puerto Banús by boat? The distance between the two marinas is roughly 4 nautical miles. At a leisurely cruising speed of 15–20 knots, it takes about 15–20 minutes to travel between them by boat. Which marina has better restaurants for pre- or post-charter meals? Both have excellent dining. Puerto Banús is known for Michelin-starred restaurants and glamorous seafood spots. Marbella Marina offers more affordable options with traditional Spanish cuisine and chiringuitos along the beach. Can I charter a boat from Marbella Marina through your company? No, all our charters start from Puerto Banús. However, you can easily take a taxi (€10–15) or a bus (line L-2) from Marbella Marina to Puerto Banús in under 20 minutes. ★★★★★ 4.9 · verified reviews From €749 2h skippered charter Instant quotes from local operators across Puerto Banús, Marbella Marina, Cabopino, Estepona & Sotogrande. 💬 Message on WhatsApp Avg reply < 5 min · No deposit until you confirm 📅 Book now Browse the full fleet → All charters include Licensed skipper & fuel Drinks: water, soft drinks, beer, white wine, cava Light snacks Insurance & safety equipment Snorkel gear & inflatables VAT 21% — no surprises

Our Sailboat Fleet in Marbella We offer two sailboats departing from Puerto Banús. For larger groups, the Lagoon 380 (11.6m, 10 pax) is a spacious catamaran ideal for day trips or overnight charters. The Dubhe (8m, 5 pax) is a classic monohull perfect for couples or small families. Both boats are maintained to high standards and include all safety equipment. Crewed vs Bareboat: What's Right for You? Crewed charter includes a licensed skipper who handles navigation, anchoring, and safety. You sit back, sip a cold beer, and enjoy the views. Perfect for first-timers or those who want a relaxing day. Bareboat rental is available for experienced sailors with a valid license. You take the helm and plan your own itinerary. We provide a briefing on local conditions, but the adventure is yours. Contact us via WhatsApp to discuss requirements. Inclusions on Every Charter All our sailboat rentals include: licensed skipper (crewed only), fuel, water, soft drinks, beer, white wine, cava, light snacks, insurance, safety equipment, and Spanish IVA (21%). No surprises—just bring your towel and sunscreen. Popular Sailing Destinations from Marbella Cabopino – 8 NM east, sandy beach and dunes. Cala del Faro – 5 NM west, quiet cove with crystal water. Estepona – 15 NM west, charming marina and old town. Sotogrande – 25 NM west, luxury marina and polo clubs. Cala Cortés – 10 NM east, secluded swimming spot. Your skipper will choose the best route based on wind and weather, ensuring a safe and memorable trip. Pricing and Booking Pricing for sailboat rentals is on request via WhatsApp. As a reference, our motor yachts start from €749/2h (Tier A). Contact us for a custom quote on the Lagoon 380 or Dubhe. No middlemen, no inflated prices. Our skippers know the coast intimately—from the Golden Mile to the cliffs of Cala del Faro. For specific availability and pricing, please contact us via WhatsApp. Can I rent a sailboat without a skipper in Marbella? Yes, bareboat rental is available if you hold a valid sailing license and have sufficient experience. However, we recommend a crewed charter for a stress-free experience, especially if you're unfamiliar with local waters. What is included in a crewed sailboat charter? Every crewed charter includes a licensed skipper, fuel, water, soft drinks, beer, white wine, cava, light snacks, insurance, safety equipment, and Spanish IVA (21%). You just bring your swimwear and sunscreen. Where can I sail from Marbella? Popular sailing destinations include Cabopino, Estepona, Sotogrande, Cala del Faro, Cala Cortés, and the coast of Gibraltar. Your skipper can tailor the itinerary based on wind conditions and your preferences. How much does a sailboat rental in Marbella cost? Pricing depends on the boat and duration. For sailboats, rates are available on request via WhatsApp. As a reference, our motor yachts start from €749/2h (Tier A). Contact us for a custom quote. What is the best time of year for sailing in Marbella? The sailing season runs from April to October, with peak conditions in June through September. Average summer temperatures are 28-32°C, and the Mediterranean sea is calm, making for ideal sailing. Do I need a license to rent a sailboat bareboat in Marbella? Yes, for bareboat rental you need a valid sailing license recognized in Spain (e.g., PER or equivalent). You must also demonstrate experience. Crewed charters require no license—just relax and enjoy. TITLE: Sunset Cruise Marbella 2026: 2-Hour Charters from €250
DESCRIPTION: Sunset cruise Marbella from €749 for 2 hours on our Astondoa 40 or Azimut 39 motor yacht. Departure 1h before sunset from Puerto Banús — skipper, drinks and VAT included.

Home › Sunset Cruise Marbella 2026: 2-Hour Charters from €250 The Marbella sunset cruise is two hours, leaves an hour before the sun touches the horizon, and ends just as the lights come on along the Golden Mile. From €250 with skipper, fuel, drinks and snacks included — and BYO cava is welcomed on every boat we work with. When the sunset cruise actually leaves Departure is 60–75 minutes before official sunset, so you're at anchor with a drink in hand when the colour starts. Local sunset times by month: Month Sunset (Marbella) Cruise departs December 18:30 17:15 March 19:30 18:15 May 21:25 20:10 June 21:55 20:40 July 21:45 20:30 August 21:10 19:55 September 20:45 19:30 October 19:45 18:30 Plan to arrive at the marina 15 minutes before departure — there's no "please wait for us" on a sunset booking when the actual sun is on a fixed schedule. The standard route From Puerto Banús, the classic 2-hour route is: Slip out of the marina mouth heading south-east, displacement speed. Cruise west along the Golden Mile — the stretch from Banús to Marbella town centre — passing Marbella Club, Nikki Beach and Ocean Club from offshore. Continue past Marbella Marina to anchor briefly off Río Real with the La Concha mountain backlit behind you. Slow turn back as the sun drops, drinks served, photos taken. Return to Puerto Banús just after twilight, marina lights coming on. From Marbella Marina the route inverts: head east to Cabopino first, anchor and return. From Cabopino, you stay east of Marbella town, with the same anchor-and-watch pattern. All three routes deliver the same sunset and very similar prices — pick by the closest marina to your hotel. Which boat fits a sunset cruise best? Couples (2): a 10 m motor yacht with a generous bow sun-pad. Intimate, fast, you can step ashore for dinner at 22:00. The romantic default. Small group (4–8): a 12 m motor yacht delivers space and the same speed. Most popular sunset booking in Marbella. Larger group (10–16): a 40+ ft sailing or power catamaran. Flat deck for golden-hour photos, more table space for catering. See catamaran rental Marbella . Party / birthday (16+): a 22 m+ yacht with a flybridge. See boat party Marbella for group cruises with music systems. For comparison with full-day options, the boat rental Marbella hub lays out every boat type side-by-side. What's included Licensed skipper for the full 2 hours Fuel for the standard route Cooler with water, soft drinks, ice Snacks (olives, almonds, crackers, fruit) Towels Use of the on-board Bluetooth sound system (BYO playlist) Not included: alcohol (BYO — cava and prosecco are the local picks), prepared dinner (add a catered platter for €25–€60 per head), and the skipper tip (€20–€40 cash is normal for a great sunset). Photography tips from local skippers Shoot the half hour BEFORE the sun drops, not after — that's when the light is on the boat and on the coast simultaneously. Stand on the bow facing land for the Golden Mile shot, or face west for the silhouette-against-sun shot. iPhones in HDR mode handle the contrast better than many people expect; bring a microfibre cloth for sea spray on the lens. We confirm the exact time the day before. How long is a typical sunset cruise? Two hours is the default. Three-hour cruises (€350) are available for groups who want a longer dinner on board. Which boat is best for sunset? 10–12 m motor yacht for couples; sail or power catamaran for 8+ guests. Avoid sportfishers and licence-free boats — they're working boats, not romantic ones. Can we have champagne and food on board? Yes, BYO welcomed on most boats (cava is the local choice). Catered platters €25–€60 per head, 24 hours notice. What if it's cloudy? Cloudy Marbella sunsets are often more dramatic than clear ones. Trip runs unless wind exceeds Force 4–5. Full refund or rebook for weather cancellations. TITLE: Terms &amp; Conditions — Boat Rental Marbella
DESCRIPTION: Terms and conditions for boat rentals booked through boatrentalinmarbella.com — booking process, pricing, payment, cancellation, weather policy, safety, liability and applicable law.

Terms & Conditions Last updated: 1 June 2026 These terms govern any booking, charter, enquiry or use of the website boatrentalinmarbella.com ("the Site") operated by Boat Rental Marbella ("we", "us"). By submitting an enquiry, accepting a quote, paying a deposit or stepping on board a chartered vessel you confirm that you have read, understood and accepted these terms. 1. About us Boat Rental Marbella is an independent charter agency based in Marbella, Andalucía, Spain. We coordinate skippered yacht, catamaran, motorboat and jet-ski charters operating out of Puerto Banús, Marbella Marina (Puerto Deportivo Virgen del Carmen), Cabopino, Estepona and Sotogrande. Charters are operated by licensed Spanish skippers and partner companies holding the appropriate maritime and commercial licences. WhatsApp / phone: +358 400 406 194 2. Booking process You send us an enquiry via the website booking form, WhatsApp, email or Instagram/Facebook DM, including the date, group size and preferred boat or experience. We reply with availability and a written quote (typically within a few hours, often within minutes during European working hours). The booking is confirmed only when (a) we send a written confirmation and (b) the agreed deposit or full payment has been received. You receive the departure address, skipper contact, meeting time and a short briefing by WhatsApp at least 24 hours before the charter. 3. Prices, payment and what's included Prices are quoted in Euros (€), include Spanish IVA (VAT, currently 21%) and — unless we explicitly state otherwise — include the licensed skipper, fuel for the standard coastal route, soft drinks and water, snorkel gear, paddleboard, towels and standard insurance. The following are typically not included unless stated: catered lunch, premium drinks, water-toy fuel (e.g. jet-ski excursion outside the charter), berthing fees in third-party ports, gratuities, and any optional add-ons (DJ, photographer, decoration). Payment options vary by operator — typically a 30–50% deposit by card, Stripe link, Revolut or SEPA bank transfer to confirm, with the balance due in cash or card on the day of the charter. Specific terms appear on the written quote. 4. Cancellation, modification and refund policy Unless your written confirmation states otherwise, the standard cancellation terms are: 7 or more days before departure — 100% refund of any amount paid. 3 to 6 days before departure — 50% refund. Less than 48 hours before departure — no refund. No-show — no refund. Date changes are free of charge if requested at least 72 hours before departure and subject to availability. 5. Weather policy The skipper is the sole authority on whether the trip can run safely. If the forecast wind exceeds Force 4–5 (approx. 20+ knots), sea state is unsafe, or a port authority issues a navigation warning, the skipper will postpone the charter — typically the evening before, or by 08:00 on the morning of the trip. In that case you are offered either: a new departure date at no extra cost (subject to availability), or a full refund of all amounts paid. Light rain alone is not a cancellation reason on the Costa del Sol. If you cancel because of weather while the skipper still considers the trip safe, the standard cancellation policy in section 4 applies. 6. Safety, conduct and the skipper's authority On board, the captain has full legal and operational authority over the vessel and its passengers under Spanish maritime law. The captain may, at their sole discretion and without refund: refuse boarding to anyone visibly intoxicated, on drugs, or behaving aggressively; alter the route, shorten the trip or return to port for safety reasons; require passengers to wear life jackets; refuse to allow swimming, jumping from the boat, or operating water toys when conditions are unsafe. All passengers must follow the captain's instructions and the on-board safety briefing. Children under 12 must wear a life jacket at all times when the boat is underway. Pets are accepted only when agreed in advance and must travel with a dog-safe life jacket supplied by the owner. 7. Behaviour, damage and cleaning Drugs of any kind are strictly forbidden on board — the captain is legally obliged to return to port and notify the Guardia Civil. The customer is liable for any damage to the vessel, fittings, water toys or third-party property caused by the customer or their guests through negligence or wilful misconduct, including but not limited to broken glassware, stained upholstery, lost or damaged snorkel gear and excessive cleaning (e.g. vomit, food spillage requiring deep clean — typically charged at €150–€500). 8. Late arrival and overruns The charter slot begins at the agreed departure time. If you arrive late, the charter still ends at the originally agreed return time and no extension or refund is owed. Extending the charter on the day is usually possible if the next slot is free — additional time is charged at 80–100% of the standard hourly rate and must be agreed with the skipper before the booked slot ends. 9. Insurance Every chartered vessel carries the third-party hull and passenger insurance required by Spanish law. This does not cover personal items (phones, cameras, jewellery, sunglasses), pre-existing medical conditions, or losses caused by your own breach of safety instructions. We strongly recommend you take out your own travel insurance with cruise/charter cover, particularly for high-value bookings or group trips. 10. Photography and content From time to time the skipper or a drone operator may take photos or short videos during the charter. By boarding you consent to non-identifying use of this material on our website and social channels (Instagram, Facebook, TikTok, YouTube). If you do not want to appear in any published material, tell the skipper before departure and we will exclude you. You may withdraw permission for previously published images by messaging us on WhatsApp at +358 400 406 194 . 11. Liability To the maximum extent permitted by Spanish law, our liability for any loss arising from your charter is limited to the total amount you paid for that charter. We are not liable for indirect or consequential losses (missed flights, accommodation costs, loss of enjoyment) caused by weather cancellations, force majeure (storms, government orders, strikes, pandemics, port closures), or third-party acts. Nothing in these terms excludes liability for death, personal injury caused by negligence, or any other liability that cannot be excluded under Spanish consumer law. 12. Affiliate disclosure Some links on this Site point to third-party operators or booking platforms. When we list a third-party operator we may receive a commission if you book through us. This never affects the price you pay and we only feature operators we would book ourselves. 13. Intellectual property All text, photos, videos and graphics on this Site are © Boat Rental Marbella or used under licence. You may share individual pages on social media and link to the Site freely. You may not republish, scrape, or use the content for AI model training without our written permission. Boat brand names (Astondoa, Azimut, Mangusta, Ferretti, etc.) belong to their respective manufacturers and are used only for descriptive reference. 14. Applicable law and jurisdiction These terms are governed by Spanish law. Any dispute between us and a consumer customer will be heard by the courts of the customer's place of residence within the EU, or by the courts of Marbella (Málaga) for non-EU customers. Consumer customers may also use the EU Online Dispute Resolution platform at ec.europa.eu/consumers/odr . 15. Yes — you board a Spanish-flagged charter, and the skipper logs passport numbers for insurance. EU national ID also works if you have dual citizenship. Can I use a UK ICC / RYA Day Skipper to drive the boat? For licence-free boats (up to 5m / 15hp): no licence needed at all. For larger boats: a UK ICC or RYA Day Skipper certificate let you charter bareboat in Spain — bring the original certificate, not a copy. TITLE: Yacht Charter Marbella 2026: Luxury Motor Yachts from €749
DESCRIPTION: Yacht charter Marbella from €749 for 2h. Our 12.5 m flybridge motor yachts (Astondoa 40 + Azimut 39) crewed by licensed skipper, departing Puerto Banús. Drinks, fuel, insurance and VAT included.

Home › Yacht Charter Marbella 2026: Luxury Motor Yachts from €749 Yacht charter in Marbella means stepping onto a 10-to-25-metre crewed motor yacht at Puerto Banús (occasionally Marbella Marina ), being handed a cold drink, and being driven up the Golden Mile coastline by a licensed skipper who knows where the wind drops in the afternoon. Prices start at €749 for a 2-hour trip and scale up to €9,500+ for a full day on a 26-metre superyacht with crew. Yacht charter Marbella prices in 2026 Crewed charter is priced by hull length, season and duration — not by guest count up to the boat's licensed capacity. The pricing grid below covers the boats that actually run from Puerto Banús and Marbella Marina, with the skipper, fuel and standard inclusions baked in. Our fleet is two 12.5 m flybridge motor yachts — same price grid above applies to both. Larger yachts (16m+) and superyachts are not currently in our fleet; if you need a bigger boat, message us and we will source one through partners. Crewed vs bareboat Roughly 95% of yacht charters from Marbella are crewed — you and your group are guests, the skipper handles the helm. Bareboat (self-drive) charter exists but requires either a Spanish PNB/PER licence or a recognised foreign equivalent (RYA Day Skipper with the ICC stamp is the most common one we see from UK customers). Even with the licence, most groups still prefer crewed because Puerto Banús's berthing manoeuvres in summer wind are not the part of your day you want to remember. Departing from Puerto Banús Puerto Banús is the natural home for yacht charter in Marbella. Yachts above 12 metres almost all berth here, and the marina infrastructure (deep water, large pontoons, walking distance restaurants for pre-board lunch) is built for charter operations. Walk down from the multi-storey carpark, your skipper meets you at the gangway with a passenger list, the safety briefing takes 90 seconds, and you're off the pontoon within 15 minutes of arrival. If you prefer something quieter, larger yachts can also pick up from Marbella Marina by arrangement (10-minute reposition motor across the bay) for the same charter price — but most guests just enjoy the Puerto Banús experience. Typical 8-hour itinerary 10:30 Boarding at Pier 3, welcome drinks, safety briefing. 11:00 Depart Puerto Banús, cruise west at 12 knots past Estepona. 12:30 Anchor off Cala del Faro, swim, paddleboard, snorkelling, lunch on board (BYO or catered). 14:30 Re-anchor at Sotogrande or push back east towards Marbella. 16:00 Optional tender ride to a beach club, or anchor near Ocean Club for a swim-up. 18:30 Return to Puerto Banús, arrive with sunset light on the Golden Mile. Skippers happily modify — heading east towards dolphin watching grounds and Cabopino is a popular variation, especially if you've done the western route before. What's included on a yacht charter Licensed skipper for the full duration Fuel for a standard coastal cruising itinerary (high-speed laps cost extra) Soft drinks, water and ice in the galley fridge Light snacks (fruit, crisps, biscuits) Snorkelling gear (masks, fins) and at least one inflatable toy (donut or SUP) Towels for every guest Marina exit and re-entry fees from the home port Not included: alcohol (BYO welcome on most boats — ask when you book), catered lunch (€25–€60 per head from the dockside caterers), berth taxes for stops at non-home marinas, and skipper tip. For the wider boat rental Marbella options including smaller and cheaper boats, compare on the main hub. Yacht charter Marbella vs. yacht charter elsewhere on the Costa del Sol The Marbella stretch — particularly Puerto Banús — concentrates more luxury motor yachts than anywhere else on the Costa del Sol. Estepona has roughly a quarter of Puerto Banús's fleet, with Sotogrande further west adding smaller numbers. If you specifically want a sailing yacht or catamaran rather than a motor yacht, see our dedicated catamaran rental Marbella page — catamarans cluster in slightly different berths. How to book a yacht charter in Marbella Message us on WhatsApp with date, duration, group size and any preferences (sun pads vs shaded cockpit, swim-heavy vs cruising, specific lunch caterer). We send back 2–3 yacht options with photos and pricing within an hour during business hours. Confirm with a 50% deposit, balance on the boarding day. Follow @boatrentalmarbella Frequently asked questions How much is a yacht charter in Marbella? Crewed motor yacht charter in Marbella costs from €749 for 2 hours on a 12.5-metre flybridge yacht (Astondoa 40 or Azimut 39), €1,299 for 4 hours and €2,299 for a full 8-hour day. The 24-metre Mangusta 80 flagship starts at €4,719 for a 4-hour minimum. Skipper, fuel, drinks and 21% IVA included. Do I need a licence to charter a yacht in Marbella? Not when you book a crewed charter — the skipper holds the licence. If you want bareboat (self-drive) on anything above 5 m / 15 hp, you need a PNB or PER Spanish licence , or a recognised foreign equivalent such as the RYA Day Skipper with the ICC stamp. What's the difference between a yacht charter and a boat rental? In Marbella, 'yacht charter' usually means a motor or sail yacht 10 metres or longer, professionally crewed, departing from a marina with full marina services. 'Boat rental' is the broader term that also covers smaller licence-free runabouts and 6-8 m day boats. Anything over €400 for 4 hours is almost always a yacht charter. Can we anchor and swim during the charter? Yes. Standard itineraries include two anchor stops for swimming and snorkelling — typical spots are Cala del Faro west of Estepona, the anchorage off Cabopino dunes, or the deeper water off Río Verde. Your skipper will pick based on wind and chop on the day. Is gratuity expected? Tipping the skipper is customary, not compulsory. €20–€50 in cash at the end of a half-day is normal; 10% of the charter price on luxury yachts is the upper-end convention. Tips are split between captain and any deckhand. On the water with us Real charters with real groups across Marbella, Puerto Banús and the Costa del Sol.
